     syllables += 1\n            prev_was_vowel = is_vowel\n        if word.endswith('e'):\n            syllables -= 1\n        if word.endswith('le') and len(word) > 2 and word[-3] not in vowels:\n            syllables += 1\n        if syllables == 0:\n            syllables = 1\n        return syllables\n    \n    total_syllables = sum(count_syllables(w) for w in words)\n    \n    # Flesch-Kincaid Grade Level\n    asl = len(words) / len(sentences)  # Average Sentence Length\n    asw = total_syllables / len(words)  # Average Syllables per Word\n    fk_grade = 0.39 * asl + 11.8 * asw - 15.59\n    \n    return max(0.0, min(12.0, fk_grade))  # Clamp to [0, 12]\n\n# Add Flesch-Kincaid to all texts\nfor item in all_texts:\n    item['flesch_kincaid'] = compute_flesch_kincaid(item['input'])\n\n# STEP 2: SBERT Embedding Computation\nfrom sentence_transformers import SentenceTransformer\n\nprint(\"Loading SBERT model...\")\nmodel = SentenceTransformer('all-MiniLM-L6-v2')\n\ndef get_sentence_embeddings(text):\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Split text into sentences and compute SBERT embeddings\\\"\\\"\\\"\n    sentences = [s.strip() + '.' for s in text.split('.') if s.strip()]\n    if len(sentences) < 2:\n        return None, None  # Skip single-sentence texts\n    embeddings = model.encode(sentences, show_progress_bar=False)\n    return sentences, embeddings\n\n# Parallel processing for efficiency\nprint(f\"Processing {len(all_texts)} texts with SBERT...\")\nwith Pool(cpu_count()) as pool:\n    embedding_results = pool.map(get_sentence_embeddings, [t['input'] for t in all_texts])\n\n# STEP 3: Cohesion Network Construction\nimport networkx as nx\nimport nltk\nfrom nltk import pos_tag, word_tokenize\n\n# Ensure NLTK data is available\ntry:\n    nltk.data.find('tokenizers/punkt')\nexcept LookupError:\n    nltk.download('punkt')\ntry:\n    nltk.data.find('taggers/averaged_perceptron_tagger')\nexcept LookupError:\n    nltk.download('averaged_perceptron_tagger')\n\ndef compute_cosine_similarity(emb1, emb2):\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Cosine similarity between two embeddings\\\"\\\"\\\"\n    return np.dot(emb1, emb2) / (np.linalg.norm(emb1) * np.linalg.norm(emb2) + 1e-8)\n\ndef get_content_words(sentence):\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Extract content words (nouns, verbs, adjectives, adverbs) using POS tagging\\\"\\\"\\\"\n    try:\n        tokens = word_tokenize(sentence.lower())\n        tagged = pos_tag(tokens)\n        content_pos = {'NN', 'VB', 'JJ', 'RB', 'NNS', 'VBP', 'JJR', 'JJS', 'NNP', 'NNPS'}\n        return set([t[0] for t in tagged if any(t[1].startswith(pos) for pos in content_pos)])\n    except:\n        return set()\n\ndef lexical_overlap(sent1, sent2):\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Compute lexical overlap ratio of content words\\\"\\\"\\\"\n    words1 = get_content_words(sent1)\n    words2 = get_content_words(sent2)\n    if not words1 or not words2:\n        return 0.0\n    overlap = len(words1.intersection(words2))\n    return overlap / max(len(words1), len(words2))\n\ndef build_cohesion_network(sentences, embeddings, use_semantic=True, use_lexical=True):\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Build cohesion network with semantic and/or lexical edges\\\"\\\"\\\"\n    n = len(sentences)\n    G = nx.Graph()\n    G.add_nodes_from(range(n))\n    \n    edges = []\n    for i in range(n):\n        for j in range(i+1, n):\n            semantic_edge = False\n            lexical_edge = False\n            sim = 0.0\n            lex_sim = 0.0\n            \n            if use_semantic:\n                sim = compute_cosine_similarity(embeddings[i], embeddings[j])\n                semantic_edge = sim > 0.5\n            \n            if use_lexical:\n                lex_sim = lexical_overlap(sentences[i], sentences[j])\n                lexical_edge = lex_sim > 0.3\n            \n            if (use_semantic and semantic_edge) or (use_lexical and lexical_edge):\n                edges.append((i, j, {'semantic': sim, 'lexical': lex_sim}))\n    \n    G.add_edges_from(edges)\n    return G, edges\n\n# STEP 4: Percolation Threshold Computation (optimized with Union-Find)\nclass UnionFind:\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Union-Find data structure for efficient component tracking\\\"\\\"\\\"\n    def __init__(self, n):\n        self.parent = list(range(n))\n        self.size = [1] * n\n        self.max_size = 1\n    \n    def find(self, x):\n        while self.parent[x] != x:\n            self.parent[x] = self.parent[self.parent[x]]\n            x = self.parent[x]\n        return x\n    \n    def union(self, x, y):\n        px, py = self.find(x), self.find(y)\n        if px == py:\n            return\n        if self.size[px] < self.size[py]:\n            px, py = py, px\n        self.parent[py] = px\n        self.size[px] += self.size[py]\n        self.max_size = max(self.max_size, self.size[px])\n\ndef compute_percolation_threshold(n_nodes, edges, n_iterations=50, alpha=0.5):\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Compute percolation threshold via random edge ordering using Union-Find\\\"\\\"\\\"\n    target_size = int(alpha * n_nodes)\n    thresholds = []\n    \n    for _ in range(n_iterations):\n        # Random edge ordering\n        shuffled_indices = np.random.permutation(len(edges))\n        \n        uf = UnionFind(n_nodes)\n        threshold = 1.0  # Default if never reaches threshold\n        \n        for idx in range(len(shuffled_indices)):\n            edge_idx = shuffled_indices[idx]\n            u, v, _ = edges[edge_idx]\n            uf.union(u, v)\n            \n            if uf.max_size >= target_size:\n                threshold = (idx + 1) / len(edges)\n                break\n        \n        thresholds.append(threshold)\n    \n    return np.mean(thresholds), np.std(thresholds)\n\n# STEP 5: Main Processing Loop\nprint(\"Computing percolation thresholds...\")\nresults = []\n\nfor idx, (text_item, emb_result) in enumerate(zip(all_texts, embedding_results)):\n    sentences, embeddings = emb_result\n    if sentences is None:\n        continue  # Skip single-sentence texts\n    \n    # Build network with both semantic and lexical edges\n    G, edges = build_cohesion_network(sentences, embeddings, use_semantic=True, use_lexical=True)\n    \n    if len(edges) == 0:\n        # No edges found, assign threshold = 1.0 (max difficulty)\n        mean_threshold, std_threshold = 1.0, 0.0\n    else:\n        # Compute percolation threshold\n        mean_threshold, std_threshold = compute_percolation_threshold(len(sentences), edges)\n    \n    # Store results\n    results.append({\n        'id': idx,\n        'dataset': text_item['dataset'],\n        'text': text_item['input'][:200] + '...' if len(text_item['input']) > 200 else text_item['input'],\n        'grade_level': text_item['output'],\n        'flesch_kincaid': text_item['flesch_kincaid'],\n        'percolation_threshold': float(mean_threshold),\n        'percolation_std': float(std_threshold),\n        'n_sentences': len(sentences),\n        'n_edges': len(edges)\n    })\n    \n    if (idx + 1) % 100 == 0:\n        print(f'Processed {idx + 1}/{len(all_texts)} texts')\n\nprint(f\"Completed processing {len(results)} texts\")\n\n# STEP 6: Evaluation Metrics\nimport scipy.stats as stats\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import LinearRegression\nfrom sklearn.metrics import mean_squared_error\n\n# Convert to arrays\npercolation_vals = np.array([r['percolation_threshold'] for r in results])\ngrade_vals = np.array([r['grade_level'] for r in results])\nfk_vals = np.array([r['flesch_kincaid'] for r in results])\n\n# Primary correlation: percolation threshold vs grade level (should be POSITIVE)\npearson_r, pearson_p = stats.pearsonr(percolation_vals, grade_vals)\nspearman_r, spearman_p = stats.spearmanr(percolation_vals, grade_vals)\n\nprint(f\"\\\\n=== MAIN RESULTS ===\")\nprint(f\"Percolation vs Grade Level: r={pearson_r:.4f}, p={pearson_p:.6f}\")\n\n# R\u00b2 and RMSE\nlr_model = LinearRegression()\nlr_model.fit(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\nr2 = lr_model.score(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\npredictions = lr_model.predict(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1))\nrmse = np.sqrt(mean_squared_error(grade_vals, predictions))\n\nprint(f\"R\u00b2 = {r2:.4f}\")\nprint(f\"RMSE = {rmse:.4f} grade levels\")\n\n# Traditional metrics baseline (Flesch-Kincaid)\nfk_pearson_r, fk_pearson_p = stats.pearsonr(fk_vals, grade_vals)\nfk_lr = LinearRegression()\nfk_lr.fit(fk_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\nfk_r2 = fk_lr.score(fk_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\n\nprint(f\"\\\\n=== BASELINE COMPARISON ===\")\nprint(f\"Flesch-Kincaid vs Grade Level: r={fk_pearson_r:.4f}, R\u00b2={fk_r2:.4f}\")\n\n# Combined model (percolation + Flesch-Kincaid)\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import Ridge\nX_combined = np.column_stack([percolation_vals, fk_vals])\ncombined_model = Ridge()\ncombined_model.fit(X_combined, grade_vals)\ncombined_r2 = combined_model.score(X_combined, grade_vals)\nprint(f\"Combined model R\u00b2 = {combined_r2:.4f} (\u0394R\u00b2 = {combined_r2 - max(r2, fk_r2):.4f})\")\n\n# STEP 7: Disaggregated Results by Dataset\nprint(f\"\\\\n=== DISAGGREGATED RESULTS ===\")\ndisaggregated = {}\nfor dataset_name in datasets:\n    subset = [r for r in results if r['dataset'] == dataset_name]\n    if not subset:\n        continue\n    subset_perc = np.array([r['percolation_threshold'] for r subset_grade)\n    fk_r, fk_p = stats.pearsonr(subset_fk, subset_grade)\n    \n    disaggregated[dataset_name] = {\n        'n': len(subset),\n        'pearson_r': float(r_val),\n        'pearson_p': print(f\"{dataset_name}: n={len(subset)}, percolation r={r_val:.3f} (p={p_val:.4f}), FK r={fk_r:.3f}\")\n\n# STEP 8: Ablation Studies\nprint(f\"\\\\n=== ABLATION STUDIES ===\")\nablation_results = {}\n\nfor ablation_name, (use_sem, use_lex) in [('semantic_only', (True, False)), ('lexical_only', (False, True)), ('full', (True, True))]:\n    ablation_thresholds = []\n    \n    # Process subset semantic_edge = False\\n            lexical_edge = False\\n            sim = 0.0\\n            lex_sim = 0.0\\n            if use_semantic:\\n                sim = sentences[j])\\n                lexical_edge = lex_sim > 0.3\\n            if (use_semantic and semantic_edge) or (use_lexical and lexical_edge):\\n                edges.append((i, j, {'semantic': sim, 'lexical': lex_sim}))\\n    return edges\\n\\n# STEP 5: Percolation Threshold with Union-Find\\nclass UnionFind:\\n    def __init__(self, n):\\n        self.parent = list(range(n))\\n        self.size = [1] * n\\n        self.max_size = 1\\n    def find(self, x):\\n        while self.parent[x] != x:\\n            self.parent[x] = self.parent[self.parent[x]]\\n            x = self.parent[x]\\n        return x\\n    def union(self, x, y):\\n        px, py = self.find(x), self.find(y)\\n        if px == py:\\n            return\\n        if self.size[px] < self.size[py]:\\n            px, py = py, px\\n        self.parent[py] = px\\n        self.size[px] += self.size[py]\\n        self.max_size = max(self.max_size, self.size[px])\\n\\ndef compute_percolation_threshold(n_nodes, edges, n_iterations=50, alpha=0.5):\\n    target_size = int(alpha * n_nodes)\\n    thresholds = []\\n    for _ in range(n_iterations):\\n        shuffled_indices = np.random.permutation(len(edges))\\n        uf = UnionFind(n_nodes)\\n        threshold = 1.0\\n        for idx in range(len(shuffled_indices)):\\n            edge_idx = shuffled_indices[idx]\\n            u, v, _ = edges[edge_idx]\\n            uf.union(u, v)\\n            if uf.max_size >= target_size:\\n                threshold = (idx + 1) / len(edges)\\n                break\\n        thresholds.append(threshold)\\n    return np.mean(thresholds), np.std(thresholds)\\n\\n# STEP 6: Main Processing Loop\\nresults = []\\nfor idx, (text_item, emb_result) in enumerate(zip(all_texts, embedding_results)):\\n    sentences, embeddings = emb_result\\n    if sentences is None:\\n        continue\\n    edges = build_cohesion_network(sentences, embeddings, use_semantic=True, use_lexical=True)\\n    if len(edges) == 0:\\n        mean_threshold, std_threshold = 1.0, 0.0\\n    else:\\n        mean_threshold, std_threshold = compute_percolation_threshold(len(sentences), edges)\\n    results.append({\\n        'id': idx,\\n        'dataset': text_item['dataset'],\\n        'text': text_item['input'][:200],\\n        'grade_level': text_item['output'],\\n        'flesch_kincaid': text_item['flesch_kincaid'],\\n        'percolation_threshold': float(mean_threshold),\\n        'percolation_std': float(std_threshold),\\n        'n_sentences': len(sentences),\\n        'n_edges': len(edges)\\n    })\\n\\n# STEP 7: Evaluation\\nimport scipy.stats as stats\\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import LinearRegression, Ridge\\nfrom sklearn.metrics import mean_squared_error\\n\\npercolation_vals = np.array([r['percolation_threshold'] for r in results])\\ngrade_vals = np.array([r['grade_level'] for r in results])\\nfk_vals = np.array([r['flesch_kincaid'] for r in results])\\n\\n# Main correlations\\npearson_r, pearson_p = stats.pearsonr(percolation_vals, grade_vals)\\nspearman_r, spearman_p = stats.spearmanr(percolation_vals, grade_vals)\\n\\n# R\u00b2 and RMSE\\nlr_model = LinearRegression()\\nlr_model.fit(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\\nr2 = lr_model.score(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\\nrmse = np.sqrt(mean_squared_error(grade_vals, lr_model.predict(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1))))\\n\\n# Baseline (Flesch-Kincaid)\\nfk_r, fk_p = stats.pearsonr(fk_vals, grade_vals)\\nfk_model = LinearRegression()\\nfk_model.fit(fk_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\\nfk_r2 = fk_model.score(fk_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\\n\\n# Combined model\\nX_combined = np.column_stack([percolation_vals, fk_vals])\\ncombined_model = Ridge()\\ncombined_model.fit(X_combined, grade_vals)\\ncombined_r2 = combined_model.score(X_combined, grade_vals)\\n\\n# STEP 8: Disaggregated Results\\nfor dataset_name in datasets:\\n    subset = [r for r in results if r['dataset'] == dataset_name]\\n    if not subset:\\n        continue\\n    subset_perc = np.array([r['percolation_threshold'] for r in subset])\\n    subset_grade = np.array([r['grade_level'] for r in subset])\\n    r_val, p_val = stats.pearsonr(subset_perc, subset_grade)\\n    print(f\\\"{dataset_name}: n={len(subset)}, r={r_val:.3f}, p={p_val:.4f}\\\")\\n\\n# STEP 9: Ablation Studies (on 500 text subset)\\nnp.random.seed(42)\\nsubset_indices = np.random.choice(len(results), min(500, len(results)), replace=False)\\nablation_results = {}\\nfor ablation_name, (use_sem, use_lex) in [('semantic_only', (True, False)), ('lexical_only', (False, True)), ('full', (True, True))]:\\n    ablation_thresholds = []\\n    for idx in subset_indices:\\n        sentences, embeddings = embedding_results[idx]\\n        if sentences is None:\\n            continue\\n        edges = build_cohesion_network(sentences, embeddings, use_semantic=use_sem, use_lexical=use_lex)\\n        if len(edges) == 0:\\n            ablation_thresholds.append(1.0)\\n        else:\\n            mean_thresh, _ = compute_percolation_threshold(len(sentences), edges, n_iterations=20)\\n            ablation_thresholds.append(mean_thresh)\\n    subset_grades = nltk.data.find('tokenizers/punkt')\nexcept LookupError:\n    nltk.download('punkt')\ntry:\n    nltk.data.find('taggers/averaged_perceptron_tagger')\nexcept LookupError:\n (np.linalg.norm(emb1) * np.linalg.norm(emb2) + 1e-8)\n\ndef get_content_words(sentence):\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Extract content words (nouns, verbs, adjectives, adverbs) using POS tagging\\\"\\\"\\\"\n    try:\n        tokens = word_tokenize(sentence.lower())\n        tagged = pos_tag(tokens)\n        content_pos = {'NN', 'VB', 'JJ', 'RB', 'NNS', 'VBP', 'JJR', 'JJS', 'NNP', 'NNPS'}\n        return set([t[0] for t in tagged if any(t[1].startswith(pos) for pos in content_pos)])\n    except:\n        return set()\n\ndef lexical_overlap(sent1, sent2):\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Compute lexical overlap ratio of content words\\\"\\\"\\\"\n    words1 = get_content_words(sent1)\n    words2 = get_content_words(sent2)\n    if not words1 or not words2:\n        return 0.0\n    overlap = len(words1.intersection(words2))\n    return overlap / max(len(words1), len(words2))\n\ndef build_cohesion_network(sentences, embeddings, use_semantic=True, use_lexical=True):\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Build cohesion network with semantic and/or lexical edges\\\"\\\"\\\"\n    n = len(sentences)\n    G = nx.Graph()\n    G.add_nodes_from(range(n))\n    \n    edges = []\n    for i in range(n):\n        for j in range(i+1, n):\n            semantic_edge = False\n            lexical_edge = False\n            sim = 0.0\n            lex_sim = 0.0\n            \n            if use_semantic:\n                sim = compute_cosine_similarity(embeddings[i], embeddings[j])\n                semantic_edge = sim > 0.5\n            \n            if use_lexical:\n                lex_sim = lexical_overlap(sentences[i], sentences[j])\n                lexical_edge = lex_sim > 0.3\n            \n            if (use_semantic and semantic_edge) or (use_lexical and lexical_edge):\n                edges.append((i, j, {'semantic': sim, 'lexical': lex_sim}))\n    \n    G.add_edges_from(edges)\n    return G, edges\n\n# STEP 4: Percolation Threshold Computation (optimized with Union-Find)\nclass UnionFind:\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Union-Find data structure for efficient component tracking\\\"\\\"\\\"\n    def __init__(self, n):\n        self.parent = list(range(n))\n        self.size = [1] * n\n        self.max_size = 1\n    \n    def find(self, x):\n        while self.parent[x] != x:\n            self.parent[x] = self.parent[self.parent[x]]\n            x = self.parent[x]\n        return x\n    \n    def union(self, x, y):\n        px, py = self.find(x), self.find(y)\n        if px == py:\n            return\n        if self.size[px] < self.size[py]:\n            px, py = py, px\n        self.parent[py] = px\n        self.size[px] += self.size[py]\n        self.max_size = max(self.max_size, self.size[px])\n\ndef compute_percolation_threshold(n_nodes, edges, n_iterations=50, alpha=0.5):\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Compute percolation threshold via random edge ordering using Union-Find\\\"\\\"\\\"\n    target_size = int(alpha * n_nodes)\n    thresholds = []\n    \n    for _ in range(n_iterations):\n        # Random edge ordering\n        shuffled_indices = np.random.permutation(len(edges))\n        \n        uf = UnionFind(n_nodes)\n        threshold = 1.0  # Default if never reaches threshold\n        \n        for idx in range(len(shuffled_indices)):\n            edge_idx = shuffled_indices[idx]\n            u, v, _ = edges[edge_idx]\n            uf.union(u, v)\n            \n            if uf.max_size >= target_size:\n                threshold = (idx + 1) / len(edges)\n                break\n        \n        thresholds.append(threshold)\n    \n    return np.mean(thresholds), np.std(thresholds)\n\n# STEP 5: Main Processing Loop\nprint(\"Computing percolation thresholds...\")\nresults = []\n\nfor idx, (text_item, emb_result) in enumerate(zip(all_texts, embedding_results)):\n    sentences, embeddings = emb_result\n    if sentences is None:\n        continue  # Skip single-sentence texts\n    \n    # Build network with both semantic and lexical edges\n    G, edges = build_cohesion_network(sentences, embeddings, use_semantic=True, use_lexical=True)\n    \n    if len(edges) == 0:\n        # No edges found, assign threshold = 1.0 (max difficulty)\n        mean_threshold, std_threshold = 1.0, 0.0\n    else:\n        # Compute percolation threshold\n        mean_threshold, std_threshold = compute_percolation_threshold(len(sentences), edges)\n    \n    # Store results\n    results.append({\n        'id': idx,\n        'dataset': text_item['dataset'],\n        'text': text_item['input'][:200] + '...' if len(text_item['input']) > 200 else text_item['input'],\n        'grade_level': text_item['output'],\n        'flesch_kincaid': text_item['flesch_kincaid'],\n        'percolation_threshold': float(mean_threshold),\n        'percolation_std': float(std_threshold),\n        'n_sentences': len(sentences),\n        'n_edges': len(edges)\n    })\n    \n    if (idx + 1) % 100 == 0:\n        print(f'Processed {idx + 1}/{len(all_texts)} texts')\n\nprint(f\"Completed processing {len(results)} texts\")\n\n# STEP 6: Evaluation Metrics\nimport scipy.stats as stats\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import LinearRegression\nfrom sklearn.metrics import mean_squared_error\n\n# Convert to arrays\npercolation_vals = np.array([r['percolation_threshold'] for r in results])\ngrade_vals = np.array([r['grade_level'] for r in results])\nfk_vals = np.array([r['flesch_kincaid'] for r in results])\n\n# Primary correlation: percolation threshold vs grade level (should be POSITIVE)\npearson_r, pearson_p = stats.pearsonr(percolation_vals, grade_vals)\nspearman_r, spearman_p = stats.spearmanr(percolation_vals, grade_vals)\n\nprint(f\"\\\\n=== MAIN RESULTS ===\")\nprint(f\"Percolation vs Grade Level: r={pearson_r:.4f}, p={pearson_p:.6f}\")\n\n# R\u00b2 and RMSE\nlr_model = LinearRegression()\nlr_model.fit(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\nr2 = lr_model.score(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\npredictions = lr_model.predict(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1))\nrmse = np.sqrt(mean_squared_error(grade_vals, predictions))\n\nprint(f\"R\u00b2 = {r2:.4f}\")\nprint(f\"RMSE = {rmse:.4f} grade levels\")\n\n# Traditional metrics baseline (Flesch-Kincaid)\nfk_pearson_r, fk_pearson_p = stats.pearsonr(fk_vals, grade_vals)\nfk_lr = LinearRegression()\nfk_lr.fit(fk_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\nfk_r2 = fk_lr.score(fk_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\n\nprint(f\"\\\\n=== BASELINE COMPARISON ===\")\nprint(f\"Flesch-Kincaid vs Grade Level: r={fk_pearson_r:.4f}, R\u00b2={fk_r2:.4f}\")\n\n# Combined model (percolation + Flesch-Kincaid)\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import Ridge\nX_combined = np.column_stack([percolation_vals, fk_vals])\ncombined_model = Ridge()\ncombined_model.fit(X_combined, grade_vals)\ncombined_r2 = combined_model.score(X_combined, grade_vals)\nprint(f\"Combined model R\u00b2 = {combined_r2:.4f} (\u0394R\u00b2 = {combined_r2 - max(r2, fk_r2):.4f})\")\n\n# STEP 7: Disaggregated Results by Dataset\nprint(f\"\\\\n=== DISAGGREGATED RESULTS ===\")\ndisaggregated = {}\nfor dataset_name in datasets:\n    subset = [r for r in results if r['dataset'] == dataset_name]\n    if not subset:\n        continue\n    subset_perc = np.array([r['percolation_threshold'] for r subset_grade)\n    fk_r, fk_p = stats.pearsonr(subset_fk, subset_grade)\n    \n    disaggregated[dataset_name] = {\n        'n': len(subset),\n        'pearson_r': float(r_val),\n        'pearson_p': print(f\"{dataset_name}: n={len(subset)}, percolation r={r_val:.3f} (p={p_val:.4f}), FK r={fk_r:.3f}\")\n\n# STEP 8: Ablation Studies\nprint(f\"\\\\n=== ABLATION STUDIES ===\")\nablation_results = {}\n\nfor ablation_name, (use_sem, use_lex) in [('semantic_only', (True, False)), ('lexical_only', (False, True)), ('full', (True, True))]:\n    ablation_thresholds = []\n    \n    # Process subset Compute correlations with grade level, evaluate predictive performance (R\u00b2, RMSE), run ablation studies, and report disaggregated results by dataset.\",\n  \"runpod_compute_profile\": \"cpu_heavy\",\n  \"implementation_pseudocode\": \"# STEP 1: Load dependency dataset\\nimport json, sys, re, numpy as np\\nfrom multiprocessing import Pool, cpu_count\\nsys.path.append('/ai-inventor/aii_data/runs/run_LOb33NvVGQcB/3_invention_loop/iter_1/gen_art/gen_art_dataset_1')\\nfrom data import load_dataset\\n\\n# Load all three datasets\\ndatasets = ['onestopenglish', 'commonlit', 'cefrsp']\\nall_texts = []\\nfor dataset_name in datasets:\\n    data = load_dataset(dataset_name)\\n    for item in data:\\n        item['dataset'] = dataset_name\\n        all_texts.append(item)\\n\\n# STEP 2: Compute Flesch-Kincaid (for circularity check)\\ndef compute_flesch_kincaid(text):\\n    sentences = [s.strip() for s in re.split(r'[.!?]+', text) if s.strip()]\\n    words = text.split()\\n    if len(sentences) == 0 or len(words) == 0:\\n        return 0.0\\n    def count_syllables(word):\\n        word = word.lower()\\n        vowels = 'aeiouy'\\n        syllables = 0\\n        prev_was_vowel = False\\n        for char in word:\\n            is_vowel = char in vowels\\n            if is_vowel and not prev_was_vowel:\\n                syllables += 1\\n            prev_was_vowel = is_vowel\\n        if word.endswith('e'):\\n            syllables -= 1\\n        if syllables == 0:\\n            syllables = 1\\n        return syllables\\n    total_syllables = sum(count_syllables(w) for w in words)\\n    asl = len(words) / len(sentences)\\n    asw = total_syllables / len(words)\\n    return max(0.0, min(12.0, 0.39 * asl + 11.8 * asw - 15.59))\\n\\nfor item in all_texts:\\n    item['flesch_kincaid'] = compute_flesch_kincaid(item['input'])\\n\\n# STEP 3: SBERT Embedding Computation\\nfrom sentence_transformers import SentenceTransformer\\nmodel = SentenceTransformer('all-MiniLM-L6-v2')\\n\\ndef get_sentence_embeddings(text):\\n    sentences = [s.strip() + '.' for s in text.split('.') if s.strip()]\\n    if len(sentences) < 2:\\n        return None, None\\n    embeddings = model.encode(sentences, show_progress_bar=False)\\n    return sentences, embeddings\\n\\nwith Pool(cpu_count()) as pool:\\n    embedding_results = pool.map(get_sentence_embeddings, [t['input'] for t in all_texts])\\n\\n# STEP 4: Cohesion Network Construction\\nimport networkx as nx\\nimport nltk\\nfrom nltk import pos_tag,        tokens = word_tokenize(sentence.lower())\\n        tagged = pos_tag(tokens)\\n        content_pos = {'NN', 'VB', 'JJ', 'RB', 'NNS', 'VBP', 'JJR', 'JJS', 'NNP', 'NNPS'}\\n        return   words2 = get_content_words(sent2)\\n    if not words1 or not words2:\\n        return 0.0\\n    return len(words1.intersection(words2)) / max(len(words1), len(words2))\\n\\ndef build_cohesion_network(sentences, embeddings, use_semantic=True, use_lexical=True):\\n    n = len(sentences)\\n    edges = []\\n    for i in range(n):\\n        for j in range(i+1, n):\\n            semantic_edge = False\\n            lexical_edge = False\\n            sim = 0.0\\n            lex_sim = 0.0\\n            if use_semantic:\\n                sim = compute_cosine_similarity(embeddings[i], embeddings[j])\\n                semantic_edge = sim > 0.5\\n            if use_lexical:\\n                lex_sim = lexical_overlap(sentences[i], sim, 'lexical': lex_sim}))\\n    return edges\\n\\n# STEP 5: Percolation Threshold with Union-Find\\nclass UnionFind:\\n    def __init__(self, n):\\n        self.parent = list(range(n))\\n        self.size = [1] * n\\n        self.max_size = 1\\n    def find(self, x):\\n        while self.parent[x] != x:\\n            self.parent[x] = self.parent[self.parent[x]]\\n            x = self.parent[x]\\n        return x\\n    def union(self, x, y):\\n        px, py = self.find(x), self.find(y)\\n        if px == py:\\n            return\\n        if self.size[px] < self.size[py]:\\n            px, py = py, px\\n        self.parent[py] = px\\n        self.size[px] += self.size[py]\\n        self.max_size = max(self.max_size, self.size[px])\\n\\ndef compute_percolation_threshold(n_nodes, edges, n_iterations=50, alpha=0.5):\\n    target_size = int(alpha * n_nodes)\\n    thresholds = []\\n    for _ in range(n_iterations):\\n        shuffled_indices = np.random.permutation(len(edges))\\n        uf = UnionFind(n_nodes)\\n        threshold = 1.0\\n        for idx in range(len(shuffled_indices)):\\n            edge_idx = shuffled_indices[idx]\\n            u, v, _ = edges[edge_idx]\\n            uf.union(u, v)\\n            if uf.max_size >= target_size:\\n                threshold = (idx + 1) / len(edges)\\n                break\\n        thresholds.append(threshold)\\n    return np.mean(thresholds), np.std(thresholds)\\n\\n# STEP 6: Main Processing Loop\\nresults = []\\nfor idx, (text_item, emb_result) in enumerate(zip(all_texts, edges)\\n    results.append({\\n        'id': idx,\\n        'dataset': text_item['dataset'],\\n        'text': text_item['input'][:200],\\n        'grade_level': text_item['output'],\\n       'n_edges': len(edges)\\n    })\\n\\n# STEP 7: Evaluation\\nimport scipy.stats as stats\\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import LinearRegression, Ridge\\nfrom sklearn.metrics import mean_squared_error\\n\\npercolation_vals = np.array([r['percolation_threshold'] for r in results])\\ngrade_vals = np.array([r['grade_level'] for r in results])\\nfk_vals = continue\\n        edges = build_cohesion_network(sentences, embeddings, use_semantic=use_sem, use_lexical=use_lex)\\n        if len(edges) == 0:\\n            ablation_thresholds.append(1.0)\\n RMSE={rmse:.3f} (target <1.5)')\\nprint(f'  4. Mean std={np.mean([r[\\\"percolation_std\\\"] for r in results]):.3f} (target <0.05)')\",\nfrom multiprocessing import Pool, cpu_count\n\nsys.path.append('/ai-inventor/aii_data/runs/run_LOb33NvVGQcB/3_invention_loop/iter_1/gen_art/gen_art_dataset_1')\nfrom data import load_dataset\n\n# Load all three datasets\ndatasets = ['onestopenglish', 'commonlit', 'cefrsp']\nall_texts = []\nfor dataset_name in datasets:\n    data = load_dataset(dataset_name)  # Returns list of {input: text, output: grade_level}\n    for item in data:\n        item['dataset'] = dataset_name\n        all_texts.append(item)\n# Total: 12,469 texts\n\n# Compute Flesch-Kincaid for circularity check and baseline comparison\ndef compute_flesch_kincaid(text):\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Compute Flesch-Kincaid Grade Level\\\"\\\"\\\"\n    sentences = [s.strip() for s in re.split(r'[.!?]+', text) if s.strip()]\n    words = text.split()\n    \n    if len(sentences) == 0 or len(words) == 0:\n        return 0.0\n    \n    # Count syllables (approximation)\n    def count_syllables(word):\n        word = word.lower()\n        syllables = 0\n        vowels = 'aeiouy'\n        prev_was_vowel = False\n        for char in word:\n            is_vowel = char in vowels\n            if is_vowel and not prev_was_vowel:\n                syllables += 1\n            prev_was_vowel = is_vowel\n        if word.endswith('e'):\n            syllables -= 1\n        if word.endswith('le') and len(word) > 2 and word[-3] not in vowels:\n            syllables += 1\n        if syllables == 0:\n            syllables = 1\n        return syllables\n    \n    total_syllables = sum(count_syllables(w) for w in words)\n    \n    # Flesch-Kincaid Grade Level\n    asl = len(words) / len(sentences)  # Average Sentence Length\n    asw = total_syllables / len(words)  # Average Syllables per Word\n    fk_grade = 0.39 * asl + 11.8 * asw - 15.59\n    \n    return max(0.0, min(12.0, fk_grade))  # Clamp to [0, 12]\n\n# Add Flesch-Kincaid to all texts\nfor item in all_texts:\n    item['flesch_kincaid'] = compute_flesch_kincaid(item['input'])\n\n# STEP 2: SBERT Embedding Computation\nfrom sentence_transformers import SentenceTransformer\n\nprint(\"Loading SBERT model...\")\nmodel = SentenceTransformer('all-MiniLM-L6-v2')\n\ndef get_sentence_embeddings(text):\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Split text into sentences and compute SBERT embeddings\\\"\\\"\\\"\n    sentences = [s.strip() + '.' for s in text.split('.') if s.strip()]\n    if len(sentences) < 2:\n        return None, None  # Skip single-sentence texts\n    embeddings = model.encode(sentences, show_progress_bar=False)\n    return sentences, embeddings\n\n# Parallel processing for efficiency\nprint(f\"Processing {len(all_texts)} texts with SBERT...\")\nwith Pool(cpu_count()) as pool:\n    embedding_results = pool.map(get_sentence_embeddings, [t['input'] for t in all_texts])\n\n# STEP 3: Cohesion Network Construction\nimport networkx as nx\nimport nltk\nfrom nltk import pos_tag, word_tokenize\n\n# Ensure NLTK data is available\ntry:\n    nltk.data.find('tokenizers/punkt')\nexcept LookupError:\n    nltk.download('punkt')\ntry:\n    nltk.data.find('taggers/averaged_perceptron_tagger')\nexcept LookupError:\n    nltk.download('averaged_perceptron_tagger')\n\ndef compute_cosine_similarity(emb1, emb2):\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Cosine similarity between two embeddings\\\"\\\"\\\"\n    return np.dot(emb1, emb2) / (np.linalg.norm(emb1) * np.linalg.norm(emb2) + 1e-8)\n\ndef get_content_words(sentence):\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Extract content words (nouns, verbs, adjectives, adverbs) using POS tagging\\\"\\\"\\\"\n    try:\n        tokens = word_tokenize(sentence.lower())\n        tagged = pos_tag(tokens)\n        content_pos = {'NN', 'VB', 'JJ', 'RB', 'NNS', 'VBP', 'JJR', 'JJS', 'NNP', 'NNPS'}\n        return set([t[0] for t in tagged if any(t[1].startswith(pos) for pos in content_pos)])\n    except:\n        return set()\n\ndef lexical_overlap(sent1, sent2):\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Compute lexical overlap ratio of content words\\\"\\\"\\\"\n    words1 = get_content_words(sent1)\n    words2 = get_content_words(sent2)\n    if not words1 or not words2:\n        return 0.0\n    overlap = len(words1.intersection(words2))\n    return overlap / max(len(words1), len(words2))\n\ndef build_cohesion_network(sentences, embeddings, use_semantic=True, use_lexical=True):\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Build cohesion network with semantic and/or lexical edges\\\"\\\"\\\"\n    n = len(sentences)\n    G = nx.Graph()\n    G.add_nodes_from(range(n))\n    \n    edges = []\n    for i in range(n):\n        for j in range(i+1, n):\n            semantic_edge = False\n            lexical_edge = False\n            sim = 0.0\n            lex_sim = 0.0\n            \n            if use_semantic:\n                sim = compute_cosine_similarity(embeddings[i], embeddings[j])\n                semantic_edge = sim > 0.5\n            \n            if use_lexical:\n                lex_sim = lexical_overlap(sentences[i], sentences[j])\n                lexical_edge = lex_sim > 0.3\n            \n            if (use_semantic and semantic_edge) or (use_lexical and lexical_edge):\n                edges.append((i, j, {'semantic': sim, 'lexical': lex_sim}))\n    \n    G.add_edges_from(edges)\n    return G, edges\n\n# STEP 4: Percolation Threshold Computation (optimized with Union-Find)\nclass UnionFind:\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Union-Find data structure for efficient component tracking\\\"\\\"\\\"\n    def __init__(self, n):\n        self.parent = list(range(n))\n        self.size = [1] * n\n        self.max_size = 1\n    \n    def find(self, x):\n        while self.parent[x] != x:\n            self.parent[x] = self.parent[self.parent[x]]\n            x = self.parent[x]\n        return x\n    \n    def union(self, x, y):\n        px, py = self.find(x), self.find(y)\n        if px == py:\n            return\n        if self.size[px] < self.size[py]:\n            px, py = py, px\n        self.parent[py] = px\n        self.size[px] += self.size[py]\n        self.max_size = max(self.max_size, self.size[px])\n\ndef compute_percolation_threshold(n_nodes, edges, n_iterations=50, alpha=0.5):\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Compute percolation threshold via random edge ordering using Union-Find\\\"\\\"\\\"\n    target_size = int(alpha * n_nodes)\n    thresholds = []\n    \n    for _ in range(n_iterations):\n        # Random edge ordering\n        shuffled_indices = np.random.permutation(len(edges))\n        \n        uf = UnionFind(n_nodes)\n        threshold = 1.0  # Default if never reaches threshold\n        \n        for idx in range(len(shuffled_indices)):\n            edge_idx = shuffled_indices[idx]\n            u, v, _ = edges[edge_idx]\n            uf.union(u, v)\n            \n            if uf.max_size >= target_size:\n                threshold = (idx + 1) / len(edges)\n                break\n        \n        thresholds.append(threshold)\n    \n    return np.mean(thresholds), np.std(thresholds)\n\n# STEP 5: Main Processing Loop\nprint(\"Computing percolation thresholds...\")\nresults = []\n\nfor idx, (text_item, emb_result) in enumerate(zip(all_texts, embedding_results)):\n    sentences, embeddings = emb_result\n    if sentences is None:\n        continue  # Skip single-sentence texts\n    \n    # Build network with both semantic and lexical edges\n    G, edges = build_cohesion_network(sentences, embeddings, use_semantic=True, use_lexical=True)\n    \n    if len(edges) == 0:\n        # No edges found, assign threshold = 1.0 (max difficulty)\n        mean_threshold, std_threshold = 1.0, 0.0\n    else:\n        # Compute percolation threshold\n        mean_threshold, std_threshold = compute_percolation_threshold(len(sentences), edges)\n    \n    # Store results\n    results.append({\n        'id': idx,\n        'dataset': text_item['dataset'],\n        'text': text_item['input'][:200] + '...' if len(text_item['input']) > 200 else text_item['input'],\n        'grade_level': text_item['output'],\n        'flesch_kincaid': text_item['flesch_kincaid'],\n        'percolation_threshold': float(mean_threshold),\n        'percolation_std': float(std_threshold),\n        'n_sentences': len(sentences),\n        'n_edges': len(edges)\n    })\n    \n    if (idx + 1) % 100 == 0:\n        print(f'Processed {idx + 1}/{len(all_texts)} texts')\n\nprint(f\"Completed processing {len(results)} texts\")\n\n# STEP 6: Evaluation Metrics\nimport scipy.stats as stats\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import LinearRegression\nfrom sklearn.metrics import mean_squared_error\n\n# Convert to arrays\npercolation_vals = np.array([r['percolation_threshold'] for r in results])\ngrade_vals = np.array([r['grade_level'] for r in results])\nfk_vals = np.array([r['flesch_kincaid'] for r in results])\n\n# Primary correlation: percolation threshold vs grade level (should be POSITIVE)\npearson_r, pearson_p = stats.pearsonr(percolation_vals, grade_vals)\nspearman_r, spearman_p = stats.spearmanr(percolation_vals, grade_vals)\n\nprint(f\"\\\\n=== MAIN RESULTS ===\")\nprint(f\"Percolation vs Grade Level: r={pearson_r:.4f}, p={pearson_p:.6f}\")\n\n# R\u00b2 and RMSE\nlr_model = LinearRegression()\nlr_model.fit(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\nr2 = lr_model.score(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\npredictions = lr_model.predict(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1))\nrmse = np.sqrt(mean_squared_error(grade_vals, predictions))\n\nprint(f\"R\u00b2 = {r2:.4f}\")\nprint(f\"RMSE = {rmse:.4f} grade levels\")\n\n# Traditional metrics baseline (Flesch-Kincaid)\nfk_pearson_r, fk_pearson_p = stats.pearsonr(fk_vals, grade_vals)\nfk_lr = LinearRegression()\nfk_lr.fit(fk_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\nfk_r2 = fk_lr.score(fk_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\n\nprint(f\"\\\\n=== BASELINE COMPARISON ===\")\nprint(f\"Flesch-Kincaid vs Grade Level: r={fk_pearson_r:.4f}, R\u00b2={fk_r2:.4f}\")\n\n# Combined model (percolation + Flesch-Kincaid)\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import Ridge\nX_combined = np.column_stack([percolation_vals, fk_vals])\ncombined_model = Ridge()\ncombined_model.fit(X_combined, grade_vals)\ncombined_r2 = combined_model.score(X_combined, grade_vals)\nprint(f\"Combined model R\u00b2 = {combined_r2:.4f} (\u0394R\u00b2 = {combined_r2 - max(r2, fk_r2):.4f})\")\n\n# STEP 7: Disaggregated Results by Dataset\nprint(f\"\\\\n=== DISAGGREGATED RESULTS ===\")\ndisaggregated = {}\nfor dataset_name in datasets:\n    subset = [r for r in results if r['dataset'] == dataset_name]\n    if not subset:\n        continue\n    subset_perc = np.array([r['percolation_threshold'] for r lex_sim = 0.0\n            if use_semantic:\n                sim = compute_cosine_similarity(embeddings[i], embeddings[j])\n                semantic_edge = sim > 0.5\n            if use_lexical:\n                lex_sim = lexical_overlap(sentences[i], sentences[j])\n                lexical_edge = lex_sim > 0.3\n            if (use_semantic and semantic_edge) or (use_lexical and lexical_edge):\n                edges.append((i, j, {'semantic': sim, 'lexical': lex_sim}))\n    return edges\n\n# STEP 5: Percolation Threshold with Union-Find\nclass UnionFind:\n    def __init__(self, n):\n        self.parent = list(range(n))\n        self.size = [1] * n\n        self.max_size = 1\n    def find(self, x):\n        while self.parent[x] != x:\n            self.parent[x] = self.parent[self.parent[x]]\n            x = self.parent[x]\n        return x\n    def union(self, x, y):\n        px, py = self.find(x), self.find(y)\n        if px == py:\n            return\n        if self.size[px] < self.size[py]:\n            px, py = py, px\n        self.parent[py] = px\n        self.size[px] += self.size[py]\n        self.max_size = max(self.max_size, self.size[px])\n\ndef compute_percolation_threshold(n_nodes, edges, n_iterations=50, alpha=0.5):\n    target_size = int(alpha * n_nodes)\n    thresholds = []\n    for _ in range(n_iterations):\n        shuffled_indices = np.random.permutation(len(edges))\n        uf = UnionFind(n_nodes)\n        threshold = 1.0\n        for idx in range(len(shuffled_indices)):\n            edge_idx = shuffled_indices[idx]\n            u, v, _ = edges[edge_idx]\n            uf.union(u, v)\n            if uf.max_size >= target_size:\n                threshold = (idx + 1) / len(edges)\n                break\n        thresholds.append(threshold)\n    return np.mean(thresholds), np.std(thresholds)\n\n# STEP 6: Main Processing Loop\nresults = []\nfor idx, (text_item, emb_result) in enumerate(zip(all_texts, embedding_results)):\n    sentences, embeddings = emb_result\n    if sentences is None:\n        continue\n    edges = build_cohesion_network(sentences, embeddings, use_semantic=True, use_lexical=True)\n    if len(edges) == 0:\n        mean_threshold, std_threshold = 1.0, 0.0\n    else:\n        mean_threshold, std_threshold = compute_percolation_threshold(len(sentences), edges)\n    results.append({\n        'id': idx,\n        'dataset': text_item['dataset'],\n        'text': text_item['input'][:200],\n        'grade_level': text_item['output'],\n        'flesch_kincaid': text_item['flesch_kincaid'],\n        'percolation_threshold': float(mean_threshold),\n        'percolation_std': float(std_threshold),\n        'n_sentences': len(sentences),\n        'n_edges': len(edges)\n    })\n\n# STEP 7: Evaluation\nimport scipy.stats as stats\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import LinearRegression, Ridge\nfrom sklearn.metrics import mean_squared_error\n\npercolation_vals = np.array([r['percolation_threshold'] for r in results])\ngrade_vals = np.array([r['grade_level'] for r in results])\nfk_vals = np.array([r['flesch_kincaid'] for r in results])\n\n# Main correlations\npearson_r, pearson_p = stats.pearsonr(percolation_vals, grade_vals)\nspearman_r, spearman_p = stats.spearmanr(percolation_vals, grade_vals)\n\n# R\u00b2 and RMSE\nlr_model = LinearRegression()\nlr_model.fit(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\nr2 = lr_model.score(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\nrmse = np.sqrt(mean_squared_error(grade_vals, lr_model.predict(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1))))\n\n# Baseline (Flesch-Kincaid)\nfk_r, fk_p = stats.pearsonr(fk_vals, grade_vals)\nfk_model = LinearRegression()\nfk_model.fit(fk_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\nfk_r2 = fk_model.score(fk_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\n\n# Combined model\nX_combined = np.column_stack([percolation_vals, fk_vals])\ncombined_model = Ridge()\ncombined_model.fit(X_combined, grade_vals)\ncombined_r2 = combined_model.score(X_combined, grade_vals)\n\n# STEP 8: Disaggregated Results\ndisaggregated = {}\nfor dataset_name in datasets:\n    subset = [r for r in results if r['dataset'] == dataset_name]\n    if not subset:\n        continue\n    subset_perc = np.array([r['percolation_threshold'] for r in subset])\n    subset_grade = np.array([r['grade_level'] for r in subset])\n    r_val, p_val = stats.pearsonr(subset_perc, subset_grade)\n    disaggregated[dataset_name] = {'n': len(subset), 'pearson_r': float(r_val), 'pearson_p': float(p_val)}\n\n# STEP 9: Ablation Studies (on 500 text subset)\nnp.random.seed(42)\nsubset_indices = np.random.choice(len(results), min(500, len(results)), replace=False)\nablation_results = {}\nfor ablation_name, (use_sem, use_lex) in [('semantic_only', (True, False)), ('lexical_only', (False, True)), ('full', (True, True))]:\n    ablation_thresholds = []\n    for idx in subset_indices:\n        sentences, embeddings = embedding_results[idx]\n        if sentences is None:\n            continue\n        edges = build_cohesion_network(sentences, embeddings, use_semantic=use_sem, use_lexical=use_lex)\n        if len(edges) == 0:\n            ablation_thresholds.append(1.0)\n        else:\n            mean_thresh, _ = compute_percolation_threshold(len(sentences), edges, n_iterations=20)\n            ablation_thresholds.append(mean_thresh)\n    subset_grades = [results[i]['grade_level'] for i in subset_indices if embedding_results[i][0] is not None]\n    ablation_thresholds = ablation_thresholds[:len(subset_grades)]\n    if len(ablation_thresholds) > 10:\n        r_val, p_val = stats.pearsonr(ablation_thresholds, subset_grades)\n        ablation_results[ablation_name] = {'pearson_r': float(r_val), 'pearson_p': float(p_val)}\n\n# STEP 10: Output Results\noutput = {\n    'method': 'percolation_threshold_readability',\n    'total_texts': len(results),\n    'overall_metrics': {\n        'pearson_r': float(pearson_r),\n        'pearson_p': float(pearson_p),\n        'spearman_r': float(spearman_r),\n        'spearman_p': float(spearman_p),\n        'r2': float(r2),\n        'rmse': float(rmse),\n        'flesch_kincaid_r': float(fk_r),\n        'flesch_kincaid_r2': float(fk_r2),\n        'combined_r2': float(combined_r2),\n        'delta_r2': float(combined_r2 - max(r2, fk_r2))\n    },\n    'disaggregated': disaggregated,\n    'ablation': ablation_results,\n    'predict_percolation': results\n}\n\nwith open('full_method_out.json', 'w') as f:\n    json.dump(output, f, indent=2)\n\nprint('Experiment complete. Success criteria:')\nprint(f'  1. Correlation r={pearson_r:.3f} (expected positive)')\nprint(f'  2. Delta R\u00b2={combined_r2 - max(r2, fk_r2):.3f} (expected >0)')\nprint(f'  3. RMSE={rmse:.3f} (target <1.5)')\nprint(f'  4. Mean std={np.mean([r[\"percolation_std\"] for r in results]):.3f} (target <0.05)')\n\"\"\",\n    \"fallback_plan\": \"If primary approach fails:\\n\\n1. SBERT memory issues: Use smaller model (paraphrase-MiniLM-L3-v2) or batch processing with smaller batch sizes\\n\\n2. NetworkX too slow for large networks: \\n   - Implement percolation using adjacency matrix operations with NumPy\\n   - Skip texts with >100 sentences (likely noise)\\n   - Use approximate percolation (check every 10 edges instead of every edge)\\n\\n3. Percolation computation too slow:\\n   - Reduce iterations from 50 to 10\\n   - Implement early stopping when giant component reaches threshold\\n   - Use Union-Find data structure for faster component tracking\\n\\n4. Output validation fails:\\n   - Ensure predict_percolation field has all required fields\\n   - Validate against schema before saving\\n   - Save partial results if full processing fails\",\n    \"testing_plan\": \"Testing strategy (gradual scaling):\\n\\n1. words = text.split()\n    if len(sentences) == 0 or len(words) == 0:\n        return 0.0\n    def count_syllables(word):\n        word = word.lower()\n        vowels = 'aeiouy'\n        syllables = 0\n        prev_was_vowel = False\n        for char in word:\n            is_vowel = char in vowels\n            if is_vowel and not prev_was_vowel:\n                syllables += 1\n            prev_was_vowel = is_vowel\n        if word.endswith('e'):\n            syllables -= 1\n        if syllables == 0:\n            syllables = 1\n        return syllables\n    total_syllables = sum(count_syllables(w) for w in words)\n    asl = len(words) / len(sentences)\n    asw = total_syllables / len(words)\n    return max(0.0, min(12.0, 0.39 * asl + 11.8 * asw - 15.59))\n\nfor item in all_texts:\n    item['flesch_kincaid'] = compute_flesch_kincaid(item['input'])\n\n# STEP 3: SBERT Embedding Computation\nfrom sentence_transformers import SentenceTransformer\nmodel = SentenceTransformer('all-MiniLM-L6-v2')\n\ndef get_sentence_embeddings(text):\n    sentences = [s.strip() + '.' for s in text.split('.') if s.strip()]\n    if len(sentences) < 2:\n        return None,    return np.dot(emb1, emb2) / (np.linalg.norm(emb1) * np.linalg.norm(emb2) + 1e-8)\n\ndef get_content_words(sentence):\n    try:\n        tokens = word_tokenize(sentence.lower())\n        tagged = pos_tag(tokens)\n        content_pos = {'NN', 'VB', 'JJ', 'RB', 'NNS', 'VBP', 'JJR', 'JJS', 'NNP', 'NNPS'}\n        return set([t[0] for t in tagged if any(t[1].startswith(pos) for pos in content_pos)])\n    except:\n        return set()\n\ndef lexical_overlap(sent1, sent2):\n    words1 = get_content_words(sent1)\n    words2 = get_content_words(sent2)\n    if not words1 or not words2:\n        return 0.0\n    return len(words1.intersection(words2)) / max(len(words1), len(words2))\n\ndef build_cohesion_network(sentences, embeddings, use_semantic=True, use_lexical=True):\n    n = len(sentences)\n    edges = []\n    for i in range(n):\n        for j in range(i+1, n):\n            semantic_edge = False\n            lexical_edge = False\n            sim = 0.0\n            lex_sim = 0.0\n            if use_semantic:\n                sim = compute_cosine_similarity(embeddings[i], embeddings[j])\n                semantic_edge = sim > 0.5\n            if use_lexical:\n            edges.append((i, j, {'semantic': sim, 'lexical': lex_sim}))\n    return edges\n\n# STEP 5: Percolation Threshold with Union-Find\nclass UnionFind:\n    def __init__(self, n):\n        self.parent = list(range(n))\n        self.size = [1] * n\n        self.max_size = 1\n    def find(self, x):\n        while self.parent[x] != x:\n            self.parent[x] = self.parent[self.parent[x]]\n            x = self.parent[x]\n        return x\n    def union(self, x, y):\n        px, py = self.find(x), self.find(y)\n        if px == py:\n            return\n        if self.size[px] < self.size[py]:\n            px, py = py, px\n        self.parent[py] = px\n        self.size[px] += self.size[py]\n        self.max_size = max(self.max_size, self.size[px])\n\ndef compute_percolation_threshold(n_nodes, edges, n_iterations=50, alpha=0.5):\n    target_size = int(alpha * n_nodes)\n    thresholds = []\n    for _ in range(n_iterations):\n        shuffled_indices = u, v, _ = edges[edge_idx]\n            uf.union(u, v)\n            if uf.max_size >= target_size:\n                threshold = (idx + 1) / len(edges)\n                break\n        thresholds.append(threshold)\n    return np.mean(thresholds), np.std(thresholds)\n\n# STEP 6: Main Processing Loop\nresults = []\nfor idx, (text_item, emb_result) in enumerate(zip(all_texts,   "file_text": "import json\n\n# Create the plan dictionary\nplan = {\n    \"title\": \"Test percolation readability on 12k texts\",\n    \"summary\": \"Implement percolation threshold readability model using SBERT embeddings on 12,469 real-world texts from three datasets (OneStopEnglish, CommonLit, CEFR-SP). Compute correlations with grade level, evaluate predictive performance (R\u00b2, RMSE), run ablation studies, and report disaggregated results by dataset.\",\n    \"runpod_compute_profile\": \"cpu_heavy\",\n    \"implementation_pseudocode\": \"# STEP 1: Load dependency dataset\\nimport json, sys, re, numpy as np\\nfrom multiprocessing import Pool, cpu_count\\nsys.path.append('/ai-inventor/aii_data/runs/run_LOb33NvVGQcB/3_invention_loop/iter_1/gen_art/gen_art_dataset_1')\\nfrom data import load_dataset\\n\\n# Load all three datasets\\ndatasets = ['onestopenglish', 'commonlit', 'cefrsp']\\nall_texts = []\\nfor dataset_name in datasets:\\n    data = load_dataset(dataset_name)\\n    for item in data:\\n        item['dataset'] = dataset_name\\n        all_texts.append(item)\\n\\n# STEP 2: Compute Flesch-Kincaid (for circularity check)\\ndef compute_flesch_kincaid(text):\\n    sentences = [s.strip() for s in re.split(r'[.!?]+', text) if s.strip()]\\n    words = text.split()\\n    if len(sentences) == 0 or len(words) == 0:\\n        return 0.0\\n    def count_syllables(word):\\n        word = word.lower()\\n        vowels = 'aeiouy'\\n        syllables = 0\\n        prev_was_vowel = False\\n        for char in word:\\n            is_vowel = char in vowels\\n            if is_vowel and not prev_was_vowel:\\n                syllables += 1\\n            prev_was_vowel = is_vowel\\n        if word.endswith('e'):\\n            syllables -= 1\\n        if syllables == 0:\\n            syllables = 1\\n        return syllables\\n    total_syllables = sum(count_syllables(w) for w in words)\\n    asl = len(words) / len(sentences)\\n    asw = total_syllables / len(words)\\n    return max(0.0, min(12.0, 0.39 * asl + 11.8 * asw - 15.59))\\n\\nfor item in all_texts:\\n    item['flesch_kincaid'] = compute_flesch_kincaid(item['input'])\\n\\n# STEP 3: SBERT Embedding Computation\\nfrom sentence_transformers import SentenceTransformer\\nmodel = SentenceTransformer('all-MiniLM-L6-v2')\\n\\ndef get_sentence_embeddings(text):\\n    sentences = [s.strip() + '.' for s in text.split('.') if s.strip()]\\n    if len(sentences) < 2:\\n        return None, None\\n    embeddings = model.encode(sentences, show_progress_bar=False)\\n    return sentences, embeddings\\n\\nwith Pool(cpu_count()) as pool:\\n    embedding_results = pool.map(get_sentence_embeddings, [t['input'] for t in all_texts])\\n\\n# STEP 4: Cohesion Network Construction\\nimport networkx as nx\\nimport nltk\\nfrom nltk import pos_tag, word_tokenize\\n\\ndef compute_cosine_similarity(emb1, emb2):\\n    return np.dot(emb1, emb2) / (np.linalg.norm(emb1) * np.linalg.norm(emb2) + 1e-8)\\n\\ndef get_content_words(sentence):\\n    try:\\n        tokens = word_tokenize(sentence.lower())\\n        tagged = pos_tag(tokens)\\n        content_pos = {'NN', 'VB', 'JJ', 'RB', 'NNS', 'VBP', 'JJR', 'JJS', 'NNP', 'NNPS'}\\n        return set([t[0] for t in tagged if any(t[1].startswith(pos) for pos in content_pos)])\\n    except:\\n        return set()\\n\\ndef lexical_overlap(sent1, sent2):\\n    words1 = get_content_words(sent1)\\n    words2 = get_content_words(sent2)\\n    if not words1 or not words2:\\n        return 0.0\\n    return len(words1.intersection(words2)) / max(len(words1), len(words2))\\n\\ndef build_cohesion_network(sentences, embeddings, use_semantic=True, use_lexical=True):\\n    n = len(sentences)\\n    edges = []\\n    for i in range(n):\\n        for j in range(i+1, n):\\n            semantic_edge = False\\n            lexical_edge = False\\n            sim = 0.0\\n            lex_sim = 0.0\\n            if use_semantic:\\n                sim = compute_cosine_similarity(embeddings[i], embeddings[j])\\n                semantic_edge = sim > 0.5\\n            if use_lexical:\\n                lex_sim = lexical_overlap(sentences[i], sentences[j])\\n                lexical_edge = lex_sim > 0.3\\n            if (use_semantic and semantic_edge) or (use_lexical and lexical_edge):\\n                edges.append((i, j, {'semantic': sim, 'lexical': lex_sim}))\\n    return edges\\n\\n# STEP 5: Percolation Threshold with Union-Find\\nclass UnionFind:\\n    def __init__(self, n):\\n        self.parent = list(range(n))\\n        self.size = [1] * n\\n        self.max_size = 1\\n    def find(self, x):\\n        while self.parent[x] != x:\\n            self.parent[x] = self.parent[self.parent[x]]\\n            x = self.parent[x]\\n        return x\\n    def union(self, x, y):\\n        px, py = self.find(x), self.find(y)\\n        if px == py:\\n            return\\n        if self.size[px] < self.size[py]:\\n            px, py = py, px\\n        self.parent[py] = px\\n        self.size[px] += self.size[py]\\n        self.max_size = max(self.max_size, self.size[px])\\n\\ndef compute_percolation_threshold(n_nodes, edges, n_iterations=50, alpha=0.5):\\n    target_size = int(alpha * n_nodes)\\n    thresholds = []\\n    for _ in range(n_iterations):\\n        shuffled_indices = np.random.permutation(len(edges))\\n        uf = UnionFind(n_nodes)\\n        threshold = 1.0\\n        for idx in range(len(shuffled_indices)):\\n            edge_idx = shuffled_indices[idx]\\n            u, v, _ = edges[edge_idx]\\n            uf.union(u, v)\\n            if uf.max_size >= target_size:\\n                threshold = (idx + 1) / len(edges)\\n                break\\n        thresholds.append(threshold)\\n    return np.mean(thresholds), np.std(thresholds)\\n\\n# STEP 6: Main Processing Loop\\nresults = []\\nfor idx, (text_item, emb_result) in enumerate(zip(all_texts, embedding_results)):\\n    sentences, embeddings = emb_result\\n    if sentences is None:\\n        continue\\n    edges = build_cohesion_network(sentences, embeddings, use_semantic=True, use_lexical=True)\\n    if len(edges) == 0:\\n        mean_threshold, std_threshold = 1.0, 0.0\\n    else:\\n        mean_threshold, std_threshold = compute_percolation_threshold(len(sentences), edges)\\n    results.append({\\n        'id': idx,\\n        'dataset': text_item['dataset'],\\n        'text': text_item['input'][:200],\\n        'grade_level': text_item['output'],\\n        'flesch_kincaid': text_item['flesch_kincaid'],\\n        'percolation_threshold': float(mean_threshold),\\n        'percolation_std': float(std_threshold),\\n        'n_sentences': len(sentences),\\n        'n_edges': len(edges)\\n    })\\n\\n# STEP 7: Evaluation\\nimport scipy.stats as stats\\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import LinearRegression, Ridge\\nfrom sklearn.metrics import mean_squared_error\\n\\npercolation_vals = np.array([r['percolation_threshold'] for r in results])\\ngrade_vals = np.array([r['grade_level'] for r in results])\\nfk_vals = np.array([r['flesch_kincaid'] for r in results])\\n\\n# Main correlations\\npearson_r, pearson_p = stats.pearsonr(percolation_vals, grade_vals)\\nspearman_r, spearman_p = stats.spearmanr(percolation_vals, grade_vals)\\n\\n# R\u00b2 and RMSE\\nlr_model = LinearRegression()\\nlr_model.fit(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\\nr2 = lr_model.score(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\\nrmse = np.sqrt(mean_squared_error(grade_vals, lr_model.predict(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1))))\\n\\n# Baseline (Flesch-Kincaid)\\nfk_r, fk_p = stats.pearsonr(fk_vals, grade_vals)\\nfk_model = LinearRegression()\\nfk_model.fit(fk_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\\nfk_r2 = fk_model.score(fk_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\\n\\n# Combined model\\nX_combined = np.column_stack([percolation_vals, fk_vals])\\ncombined_model = Ridge()\\ncombined_model.fit(X_combined, grade_vals)\\ncombined_r2 = combined_model.score(X_combined, grade_vals)\\n\\n# STEP 8: Disaggregated Results\\nfor dataset_name in datasets:\\n    subset = [r for r in results if r['dataset'] == dataset_name]\\n    if not subset:\\n        continue\\n    subset_perc = np.array([r['percolation_threshold'] for r in subset])\\n    subset_grade = np.array([r['grade_level'] for r in subset])\\n    r_val, p_val = stats.pearsonr(subset_perc, subset_grade)\\n    print(f\\\"{dataset_name}: n={len(subset)}, r={r_val:.3f}, p={p_val:.4f}\\\")\\n\\n# STEP 9: Ablation Studies (on 500 text subset)\\nnp.random.seed(42)\\nsubset_indices = np.random.choice(len(results), min(500, len(results)), replace=False)\\nablation_results = {}\\nfor ablation_name, (use_sem, use_lex) in [('semantic_only', (True, False)), ('lexical_only', (False, True)), ('full', (True, True))]:\\n    ablation_thresholds = []\\n    for idx in subset_indices:\\n        sentences, embeddings = embedding_results[idx]\\n        if sentences is None:\\n            continue\\n        edges = build_cohesion_network(sentences, embeddings, use_semantic=use_sem, use_lexical=use_lex)\\n        if len(edges) == 0:\\n            ablation_thresholds.append(1.0)\\n        else:\\n            mean_thresh, _ = compute_percolation_threshold(len(sentences), edges, n_iterations=20)\\n            ablation_thresholds.append(mean_thresh)\\n    subset_grades = [results[i]['grade_level'] for i in subset_indices if embedding_results[i][0] is not None]\\n    ablation_thresholds = ablation_thresholds[:len(subset_grades)]\\n    if len(ablation_thresholds) > 10:\\n        r_val, p_val = stats.pearsonr(ablation_thresholds, subset_grades)\\n        ablation_results[ablation_name] = {'pearson_r': float(r_val), 'pearson_p': float(p_val)}\\n\\n# STEP 10: Output Results\\noutput = {\\n    'method': 'percolation_threshold_readability',\\n    'total_texts': len(results),\\n    'overall_metrics': {\\n        'pearson_r': float(pearson_r),\\n        'pearson_p': float(pearson_p),\\n        'spearman_r': float(spearman_r),\\n        'spearman_p': float(spearman_p),\\n        'r2': float(r2),\\n        'rmse': float(rmse),\\n        'flesch_kincaid_r': float(fk_r),\\n        'flesch_kincaid_r2': float(fk_r2),\\n        'combined_r2': float(combined_r2),\\n        'delta_r2': float(combined_r2 - max(r2, fk_r2))\\n    },\\n    'disaggregated': {ds: {'n': len([r for r in results if r['dataset']==ds])} for ds in datasets},\\n    'ablation': ablation_results,\\n    'predict_percolation': results\\n}\\n\\nwith open('full_method_out.json', 'w') as f:\\n    json.dump(output, f, indent=2)\\n\\nprint('Experiment complete. Success criteria:')\\nprint(f'  1. Correlation r={pearson_r:.3f} (expected positive)')\\nprint(f'  2. Delta R\u00b2={combined_r2 - max(r2, fk_r2):.3f} (expected >0)')\\nprint(f'  3. RMSE={rmse:.3f} (target <1.5)')\\nprint(f'  4. Mean std={np.mean([r[\\\"percolation_std\\\"] for r in results]):.3f} (target <0.05)')\",\n    \"fallback_plan\": \"If primary approach fails:\\n\\n1. SBERT memory issues: Use smaller model (paraphrase-MiniLM-L3-v2) or batch processing with smaller batch sizes\\n\\n2. NetworkX too slow for large networks: \\n   - Implement percolation using adjacency matrix operations with NumPy\\n   - Skip texts with >100 sentences (likely noise)\\n   - Use approximate percolation (check every 10 edges instead of every edge)\\n\\n3. Percolation computation too slow:\\n   - Reduce iterations from 50 to 10\\n   - Implement early stopping when giant component reaches threshold\\n   - Use Union-Find data structure for faster component tracking\\n\\n4. 'aeiouy'\\n        syllables = 0\\n        prev_was_vowel = False\\n        for char in word:\\n            is_vowel = char in vowels\\n            if is_vowel and not prev_was_vowel:\\n                syllables += 1\\n            prev_was_vowel = is_vowel\\n        if word.endswith('e'):\\n            syllables -= 1\\n        if syllables == 0:\\n            syllables = 1\\n        return syllables\\n    total_syllables = sum(count_syllables(w) for w in words)\\n    asl = len(words) / len(sentences)\\n    asw = total_syllables / len(words)\\n    return max(0.0, min(12.0, 0.39 * asl + 11.8 * asw - 15.59))\\n\\nfor item in all_texts:\\n    item['flesch_kincaid'] = compute_flesch_kincaid(item['input'])\\n\\n# STEP 3: SBERT Embedding Computation\\nfrom sentence_transformers import SentenceTransformer\\nmodel = SentenceTransformer('all-MiniLM-L6-v2')\\n\\ndef get_sentence_embeddings(text):\\n    sentences = [s.strip() + '.' for s in text.split('.') if s.strip()]\\n    if len(sentences) < 2:\\n        return None, None\\n    embeddings = model.encode(sentences, show_progress_bar=False)\\n    return sentences, embeddings\\n\\nwith Pool(cpu_count()) as pool:\\n    embedding_results = pool.map(get_sentence_embeddings, [t['input'] for t in all_texts])\\n\\n# STEP 4: Cohesion Network Construction\\nimport networkx as nx\\nimport nltk\\nfrom nltk import pos_tag, word_tokenize\\n\\ndef compute_cosine_similarity(emb1, emb2):\\n    return np.dot(emb1, emb2) / (np.linalg.norm(emb1) * np.linalg.norm(emb2) + 1e-8)\\n\\ndef get_content_words(sentence):\\n    try:\\n        tokens = word_tokenize(sentence.lower())\\n        tagged = pos_tag(tokens)\\n        content_pos = {'NN', 'VB', 'JJ', 'RB', 'NNS', 'VBP', 'JJR', 'JJS', 'NNP', 'NNPS'}\\n        return set([t[0] for t in tagged if any(t[1].startswith(pos) for pos in content_pos)])\\n    except:\\n        return set()\\n\\ndef lexical_overlap(sent1, sent2):\\n    words1 = get_content_words(sent1)\\n    words2 = get_content_words(sent2)\\n    if not words1 or not words2:\\n        return 0.0\\n    return len(words1.intersection(words2)) / max(len(words1), len(words2))\\n\\ndef build_cohesion_network(sentences, embeddings, use_semantic=True, use_lexical=True):\\n    n = len(sentences)\\n    edges = []\\n    for i in range(n):\\n        for j in range(i+1, n):\\n            semantic_edge = False\\n            lexical_edge = False\\n            sim = 0.0\\n            lex_sim = 0.0\\n            if use_semantic:\\n                sim = compute_cosine_similarity(embeddings[i], embeddings[j])\\n                semantic_edge = sim > 0.5\\n            if use_lexical:\\n                lex_sim = lexical_overlap(sentences[i], sentences[j])\\n                lexical_edge = lex_sim > 0.3\\n            if (use_semantic and semantic_edge) or (use_lexical and lexical_edge):\\n                edges.append((i, j, {'semantic': sim, 'lexical': lex_sim}))\\n    return edges\\n\\n# STEP 5: Percolation Threshold with Union-Find\\nclass UnionFind:\\n    def __init__(self, n):\\n        self.parent = list(range(n))\\n        self.size = [1] * n\\n        self.max_size = 1\\n    def find(self, x):\\n        while self.parent[x] != x:\\n            self.parent[x] = self.parent[self.parent[x]]\\n            x = self.parent[x]\\n        return x\\n    def union(self, x, y):\\n        px, py = self.find(x), self.find(y)\\n        if px == py:\\n            return\\n        if self.size[px] < self.size[py]:\\n            px, py = py, px\\n        self.parent[py] = px\\n        self.size[px] += self.size[py]\\n        self.max_size = max(self.max_size, self.size[px])\\n\\ndef compute_percolation_threshold(n_nodes, edges, n_iterations=50, alpha=0.5):\\n    target_size = int(alpha * n_nodes)\\n    thresholds = []\\n    for _ in range(n_iterations):\\n        shuffled_indices = np.random.permutation(len(edges))\\n        uf = UnionFind(n_nodes)\\n        threshold = 1.0\\n        for idx in range(len(shuffled_indices)):\\n            edge_idx = shuffled_indices[idx]\\n            u, v, _ = edges[edge_idx]\\n            uf.union(u, v)\\n            if uf.max_size >= target_size:\\n                threshold = (idx + 1) / len(edges)\\n                break\\n        thresholds.append(threshold)\\n    return np.mean(thresholds), np.std(thresholds)\\n\\n# STEP 6: Main Processing Loop\\nresults = []\\nfor idx, (text_item, emb_result) in enumerate(zip(all_texts, embedding_results)):\\n    sentences, embeddings = emb_result\\n    if sentences is None:\\n        continue\\n    edges = build_cohesion_network(sentences, embeddings, use_semantic=True, use_lexical=True)\\n    if len(edges) == 0:\\n        mean_threshold, std_threshold = 1.0, 0.0\\n    else:\\n        mean_threshold, std_threshold = compute_percolation_threshold(len(sentences), edges)\\n    results.append({\\n        'id': idx,\\n        'dataset': text_item['dataset'],\\n        'text': text_item['input'][:200],\\n        'grade_level': text_item['output'],\\n        'flesch_kincaid': text_item['flesch_kincaid'],\\n        'percolation_threshold': float(mean_threshold),\\n        'percolation_std': float(std_threshold),\\n        'n_sentences': len(sentences),\\n        'n_edges': len(edges)\\n    })\\n\\n# STEP 7: Evaluation\\nimport scipy.stats as stats\\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import LinearRegression, Ridge\\nfrom sklearn.metrics import mean_squared_error\\n\\npercolation_vals = np.array([r['percolation_threshold'] for r in results])\\ngrade_vals = np.array([r['grade_level'] for r in results])\\nfk_vals = np.array([r['flesch_kincaid'] for r in results])\\n\\n# Main correlations\\npearson_r, pearson_p = stats.pearsonr(percolation_vals, grade_vals)\\nspearman_r, spearman_p = stats.spearmanr(percolation_vals, grade_vals)\\n\\n# R\u00b2 and RMSE\\nlr_model = LinearRegression()\\nlr_model.fit(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\\nr2 = lr_model.score(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\\nrmse = np.sqrt(mean_squared_error(grade_vals, lr_model.predict(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1))))\\n\\n# Baseline (Flesch-Kincaid)\\nfk_r, fk_p = stats.pearsonr(fk_vals, grade_vals)\\nfk_model = LinearRegression()\\nfk_model.fit(fk_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\\nfk_r2 = fk_model.score(fk_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\\n\\n# Combined model\\nX_combined = np.column_stack([percolation_vals, fk_vals])\\ncombined_model = Ridge()\\ncombined_model.fit(X_combined, grade_vals)\\ncombined_r2 = combined_model.score(X_combined, grade_vals)\\n\\n# STEP 8: Disaggregated Results\\nfor dataset_name in datasets:\\n    subset = [r for r in results if r['dataset'] == dataset_name]\\n    if not subset:\\n        continue\\n    subset_perc = np.array([r['percolation_threshold'] for r in subset])\\n    subset_grade = np.array([r['grade_level'] for r in subset])\\n    r_val, p_val = stats.pearsonr(subset_perc, subset_grade)\\n    print(f\\\"{dataset_name}: n={len(subset)}, r={r_val:.3f}, p={p_val:.4f}\\\")\\n\\n# STEP 9: Ablation Studies (on 500 text subset)\\nnp.random.seed(42)\\nsubset_indices = np.random.choice(len(results), min(500, len(results)), replace=False)\\nablation_results = {}\\nfor ablation_name, (use_sem, use_lex) in [('semantic_only', (True, False)), ('lexical_only', (False, True)), ('full', (True, True))]:\\n    ablation_thresholds = []\\n    for idx in subset_indices:\\n        sentences, embeddings = embedding_results[idx]\\n        if sentences is None:\\n            continue\\n        edges = build_cohesion_network(sentences, embeddings, use_semantic=use_sem, use_lexical=use_lex)\\n        if len(edges) == 0:\\n            ablation_thresholds.append(1.0)\\n        else:\\n            mean_thresh, _ = compute_percolation_threshold(len(sentences), edges, n_iterations=20)\\n            ablation_thresholds.append(mean_thresh)\\n    subset_grades = [results[i]['grade_level'] for i in subset_indices if embedding_results[i][0] is not None]\\n    ablation_thresholds = ablation_thresholds[:len(subset_grades)]\\n    if len(ablation_thresholds) > 10:\\n        r_val, p_val = stats.pearsonr(ablation_thresholds, subset_grades)\\n        ablation_results[ablation_name] = {'pearson_r': float(r_val), 'pearson_p': float(p_val)}\\n\\n# STEP 10: Output Results\\noutput = {\\n    'method': 'percolation_threshold_readability',\\n    'total_texts': len(results),\\n    'overall_metrics': {\\n        'pearson_r': float(pearson_r),\\n        'pearson_p': float(pearson_p),\\n        'spearman_r': float(spearman_r),\\n        'spearman_p': float(spearman_p),\\n        'r2': float(r2),\\n        'rmse': float(rmse),\\n        'flesch_kincaid_r': float(fk_r),\\n        'flesch_kincaid_r2': float(fk_r2),\\n        'combined_r2': float(combined_r2),\\n        'delta_r2': float(combined_r2 - max(r2, fk_r2))\\n    },\\n    'disaggregated': {ds: {'n': len([r for r in results if r['dataset']==ds])} for ds in datasets},\\n    'ablation': ablation_results,\\n    'predict_percolation': results\\n}\\n\\nwith Success criteria:')\\nprint(f'  1. Correlation r={pearson_r:.3f} (expected positive)')\\nprint(f'  2. Delta R\u00b2={combined_r2 - max(r2, fk_r2):.3f} (expected >0)')\\nprint(f'  3. RMSE={rmse:.3f} (target <1.5)')\\nprint(f'  4. Mean std={np.mean([r[\\\"percolation_std\\\"] for r in results]):.3f} (target <0.05)')\",\n    \"fallback_plan\": \"If primary approach fails:\\n\\n1. SBERT memory issues: Use smaller model (paraphrase-MiniLM-L3-v2) or batch processing with smaller batch sizes\\n\\n2. NetworkX too slow for large networks: \\n   - Implement percolation using adjacency matrix operations with NumPy\\n   - Skip texts with >100 sentences (likely noise)\\n   - Use approximate percolation (check every 10 edges instead of every edge)\\n\\n3. self.parent[self.parent[x]]\n            x = self.parent[x]\n        return x\n    def union(self, x, y):\n        px, py = self.find(x), self.find(y)\n        if px == py:\n            return\n compute_percolation_threshold(n_nodes, edges, n_iterations=50, alpha=0.5):\n    target_size = int(alpha * n_nodes)\n    thresholds = []\n    for _ in range(n_iterations):\n        shuffled_indices = np.random.permutation(len(edges))\n        uf = UnionFind(n_nodes)\n        threshold = 1.0\n        for idx in range(len(shuffled_indices)):\n            edge_idx = shuffled_indices[idx]\n            u, v, _ = edges[edge_idx]\n            uf.union(u, v)\n            if uf.max_size >= target_size:\n                threshold = (idx + 1) / len(edges)\n                break\n        thresholds.append(threshold)\n    return np.mean(thresholds), np.std(thresholds)\n\n# STEP 6: Main Processing Loop\nresults = []\nfor idx, (text_item, emb_result) in enumerate(zip(all_texts, embedding_results)):\n    sentences, embeddings = emb_result\n    if sentences is None:\n        continue\n    edges = build_cohesion_network(sentences, embeddings, use_semantic=True, use_lexical=True)\n    if len(edges) == 0:\n        mean_threshold, std_threshold = 1.0, 0.0\n    else:\n        mean_threshold, std_threshold = compute_percolation_threshold(len(sentences), edges)\n    results.append({\n        'id': idx,\n        'dataset': text_item['dataset'],\n        'text': text_item['input'][:200],\n        'grade_level': text_item['output'],\n        'flesch_kincaid': text_item['flesch_kincaid'],\n        'percolation_threshold': float(mean_threshold),\n        'percolation_std': float(std_threshold),\n        'n_sentences': len(sentences),\n        'n_edges': len(edges)\n    })\n\n# STEP 7: Evaluation\nimport scipy.stats as stats\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import LinearRegression, Ridge\nfrom sklearn.metrics import mean_squared_error\n\npercolation_vals = np.array([r['percolation_threshold'] for r in results])\ngrade_vals = np.array([r['grade_level'] for r in results])\nfk_vals = np.array([r['flesch_kincaid'] for r in results])\n\n# Main correlations\npearson_r, pearson_p = stats.pearsonr(percolation_vals, grade_vals)\nspearman_r, spearman_p = stats.spearmanr(percolation_vals, grade_vals)\n\n# R2 and RMSE\nlr_model = LinearRegression()\nlr_model.fit(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\nr2 = lr_model.score(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\nrmse = np.sqrt(mean_squared_error(grade_vals, lr_model.predict(percolation_vals.reshape(-1, 1))))\n\n# Baseline (Flesch-Kincaid)\nfk_r, fk_p = stats.pearsonr(fk_vals, grade_vals)\nfk_model = LinearRegression()\nfk_model.fit(fk_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\nfk_r2 = fk_model.score(fk_vals.reshape(-1, 1), grade_vals)\n\n# Combined model\nX_combined = np.column_stack([percolation_vals, fk_vals])\ncombined_model = Ridge()\ncombined_model.fit(X_combined, grade_vals)\ncombined_r2 = combined_model.score(X_combined, grade_vals)\n\n# STEP 8: Disaggregated Results\nfor dataset_name in datasets:\n    subset = [r for r in results if r['dataset'] == dataset_name]\n    if not subset:\n        continue\n    subset_perc = np.array([r['percolation_threshold'] for r in subset])\n    subset_grade = np.array([r['grade_level'] for r in subset])\n    r_val, p_val = stats.pearsonr(subset_perc, subset_grade)\n    print(f\"{dataset_name}: n={len(subset)}, r={r_val:.3f}, p={p_val:.4f}\")\n\n# STEP 9: Ablation Studies (on 500 text subset)\nnp.random.seed(42)\nsubset_indices = np.random.choice(len(results), min(500, len(results)), replace=False)\nablation_results = {}\nfor ablation_name, (use_sem, use_lex) in [('semantic_only', (True, False)), ('lexical_only', (False, True)), ('full', (True, True))]:\n    ablation_thresholds = []\n    for idx in subset_indices:\n        sentences, embeddings = embedding_results[idx]\n        if sentences is None:\n            continue\n        edges = build_cohesion_network(sentences, embeddings, use_semantic=use_sem, use_lexical=use_lex)\n        if len(edges) == 0:\n            ablation_thresholds.append(1.0)\n        else:\n            mean_thresh, _ = compute_percolation_threshold(len(sentences), edges, n_iterations=20)\n            ablation_thresholds.append(mean_thresh)\n    subset_grades = [results[i]['grade_level'] for i in subset_indices if embedding_results[i][0] is not None]\n    ablation_thresholds = ablation_thresholds[:len(subset_grades)]\n    if len(ablation_thresholds) > 10:\n        r_val, p_val = stats.pearsonr(ablation_thresholds, subset_grades)\n        ablation_results[ablation_name] = {'pearson_r': float(r_val), 'pearson_p': float(p_val)}\n\n# STEP 10: Output Results\noutput = {\n    'method': 'percolation_threshold_readability',\n    'total_texts': len(results),\n    'overall_metrics': {\n        'pearson_r': float(pearson_r),\n        'pearson_p': float(pearson_p),\n        'spearman_r': float(spearman_r),\n        'spearman_p': float(spearman_p),\n        'r2': float(r2),\n        'rmse': float(rmse),\n        'flesch_kincaid_r': float(fk_r),\n        'flesch_kincaid_r2': float(fk_r2),\n        'combined_r2': float(combined_r2),\n        'delta_r2': float(combined_r2 - max(r2, fk_r2))\n    },\n    'disaggregated': {ds: {'n': len([r for r in results if r['dataset']==ds])} for ds in datasets},\n    'ablation': ablation_results,\n    'predict_percolation': results\n}\n\nwith open('full_method_out.json', 'w') as f:\n    json.dump(output, f, indent=2)\n\nprint('Experiment complete. Success criteria:')\nprint(f'  1. Correlation r={pearson_r:.3f} (expected positive)')\nprint(f'  2. Delta R2={combined_r2 - max(r2, fk_r2):.3f} (expected >0)')\nprint(f'  3. RMSE={rmse:.3f} (target <1.5)')\n\"\"\",\n    \"fallback_plan\": \"If primary approach fails:\\n\\n1. SBERT memory issues: Use smaller model (paraphrase-MiniLM-L3-v2) or batch processing with smaller batch sizes\\n\\n2. NetworkX too slow for large networks: \\n   - Implement percolation using adjacency matrix operations with NumPy\\n   - Skip texts with >100 sentences (likely noise)\\n   - Use approximate percolation (check every 10 edges instead of every edge)\\n\\n3. Output validation fails:\\n   - Ensure predict_percolation field has all required fields\\n   - Validate against schema before saving\\n   - Save partial results if full processing fails\",\n    \"testing_plan\": \"Testing strategy (gradual scaling):\\n\\n1. UNIT TESTS (before full run):\\n   - Test SBERT embedding on 5 sample sentences\\n   - Test network construction on 3-sample text (5 sentences)\\n   - Test percolation threshold on small network (10 nodes)\\n   - Verify cosine similarity computation\\n   - Verify lexical overlap computation\\n\\n2. words = text.split()\n    if len(sentences) == 0 or len(words) == 0:\n        return 0.0\n    def count_syllables(word):\n        word = word.lower()\n        vowels = 'aeiouy'\n        syllables = 0\n        prev_was_vowel = False\n        for char in word:\n            is_vowel = char in vowels\n            if is_vowel and not prev_was_vowel:\n                syllables += 1\n            prev_was_vowel = is_vowel\n        if word.endswith('e'):\n            syllables -= 1\n        if syllables == 0:\n            syllables = 1\n        return syllables\n    total_syllables =    return np.dot(emb1, emb2) / (np.linalg.norm(emb1) * np.linalg.norm(emb2) + 1e-8)\n\ndef get_content_words(sentence):\n    try:\n        tokens = word_tokenize(sentence.lower())\n        tagged = pos_tag(tokens)\n        content_pos = {'NN', 'VB', 'JJ', 'RB', 'NNS', 'VBP', 'JJR', 'JJS', 'NNP', 'NNPS'}\n        return set([t[0] for t in tagged if any(t[1].startswith(pos) for pos in words2:\n        return 0.0\n    return len(words1.intersection(words2)) / max(len(words1), len(words2))\n\ndef build_cohesion_network(sentences, embeddings, use_semantic=True, use_lexical=True):\n    n = len(sentences)\n    edges = []\n    for i in range(n):\n        for j in range(i+1, n):\n            semantic_edge = False\n            lexical_edge = False\n            sim = 0.0\n            lex_sim = 0.0\n            if use_semantic:\n                sim = compute_cosine_similarity(embeddings[i], embeddings[j])\n                semantic_edge = sim > 0.5\n            if use_lexical:\n                lex_sim = lexical_overlap(sentences[i], sentences[j])\n                lexical_edge = lex_sim > 0.3\n            if (use_semantic and semantic_edge) or (use_lexical and lexical_edge):\n                edges.append((i, j, {'semantic': sim, 'lexical': lex_sim}))\n    return edges\n\n# STEP 5: Percolation Threshold with Union-Find\nclass UnionFind:\n    def __init__(self, n):\n        self.parent = list(range(n))\n        self.size = [1] * n\n        self.max_size = 1\n    def find(self, x):\n        while self.parent[x] != x:\n            self.parent[x] = self.parent[self.parent[x]]\n            x = self.parent[x]\n        return x\n    def union(self, x, y):\n        px, py = self.find(x), self.find(y)\n        if px == py:\n            return\n        if self.size[px] < self.size[py]:\n            px, py = py, px\n        self.parent[py] = px\n        self.size[px] += self.size[py]\n        self.max_size = max(self.max_size, self.size[px])\n\ndef compute_percolation_threshold(n_nodes, edges, n_iterations=50, alpha=0.5):\n    target_size = int(alpha * n_nodes)\n    thresholds = []\n    for _ in range(n_iterations):\n        shuffled_indices = u, v, _ = edges[edge_idx]\n            uf.union(u, v)\n            if uf.max_size >= target_size:\n                threshold = (idx + 1) / len(edges)\n                break\n        thresholds.append(threshold)\n    return np.mean(thresholds), np.std(thresholds)\n\n# STEP 6: Main Processing Loop\nresults = []\nfor idx, (text_item, emb_result) in enumerate(zip(all_texts,
